[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write operation that underflows a stack-allocated buffer. This is a memory[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability is a stack-buffer-overflow in `dissect_ber_GeneralString` at line[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3194[0m[39m of `epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c`. The function has two critical bugs:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m3188[0m[39m - Reading from Wrong Location**: [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` reads from the original tvb at the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpost-parsing offset[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - After `dissect_ber_restricted_string` returns at line [0m[1;36m3179[0m[39m, `offset` points [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAFTER the string data[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This reads arbitrary packet data [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m0xc6[0m[39m = [0m[1;36m198[0m[39m from fuzzer input[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m instead [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mof the actual string length[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m - Unchecked Buffer Write**: [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;` uses the incorrectly-read value to index the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When `tvb_len >= name_len` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., [0m[1;36m198[0m[39m >= [0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, this writes beyond the [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The AddressSanitizer reports a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write at offset [0m[1;36m159[0m[39m, which is [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m byte [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbefore the buffer start at offset [0m[1;36m160[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Insights[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `out_tvb` returned by `dissect_ber_restricted_string` contains the correctly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextracted string data[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The actual string length should be obtained from `out_tvb` using [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A safe implementation exists but is disabled [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3040[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3101[0m[39m, wrapped in `#if [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0[0m[39m`[0m[33m...[0m[39m`#endif`[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The safe pattern: clamp length to `max_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m`, then place null terminator at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`str[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlen[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Code Flow Analysis[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `try_dissect_unknown_ber` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m814[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allocates `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m80[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` on stack [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m825[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m935[0m[39m: Calls `dissect_ber_GeneralString` with buffer and size [0m[1;36m80[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m3179[0m[39m: `dissect_ber_restricted_string` parses BER encoding, creates [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`out_tvb` with string data[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m3188[0m[39m: **BUG** - reads wrong data from post-parse offset[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Line [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m: **OVERFLOW** - writes using unchecked arbitrary value[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Patch Location[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: `epan/dissectors/packet-ber.c`  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Function**: `dissect_ber_GeneralString` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3172[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3199[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Lines to Modify**: [0m[1;36m3188[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3194[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Detailed Fix Steps[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Replace line [0m[1;36m3188[0m[39m** - Get actual string length from `out_tvb`:[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change from: `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_get_uint8[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Change to: `tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rationale: `out_tvb` contains the parsed string data with correct length[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Insert length clamping after line [0m[1;36m3188[0m[39m** - Ensure bounds safety:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Add: `if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m tvb_len = name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m`[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rationale: Prevents writing beyond buffer bounds, matches safe pattern at line[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3091[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Simplify lines [0m[1;36m3189[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3193[0m[39m** - Use single memcpy with clamped length:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the conditional memcpy with: `[0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rationale: After clamping, `tvb_len` is always safe; no need for branching[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Keep line [0m[1;36m3194[0m[39m** - Null terminate at safe position:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No change needed: `name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;`[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rationale: After clamping, `tvb_len < name_len`, so this write is always [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin bounds[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Details[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe corrected code block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3187[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3195[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m should be:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    tvb_len = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Get actual length from [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout_tvb[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mtvb_len >= name_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Clamp to buffer size[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        tvb_len = name_len - [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mout_tvb, [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint8_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mname_string, [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Copy safe amount[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    name_string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtvb_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;                   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Null terminate at safe [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mposition[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Fix Is Optimal[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Correctness**: Uses the actual parsed string length from `out_tvb` instead of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marbitrary packet data[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Safety**: Clamping ensures all buffer accesses are within bounds[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Consistency**: Follows the proven safe pattern from the disabled [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3094[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Impact**: Only modifies the buggy section without affecting other [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preservation**: Maintains the same API and behavior for all callers[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preserved Logic[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The function signature remains unchanged[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The BER parsing via `dissect_ber_restricted_string` is preserved[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Protocol tree building behavior is unaffected[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Return value and offset tracking remain the same[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing callers [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., line [0m[1;36m935[0m[39m in `try_dissect_unknown_ber`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m work without [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodification[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Potential Side Effect**: Long strings [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>= [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will be truncated to [0m[1;36m79[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacters plus null terminator[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: This is the correct behavior:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The caller allocates an [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m-byte buffer expecting truncation if needed[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The disabled safe implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3091[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m shows this is intended behavior[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- BER protocol allows strings of arbitrary length; truncation is necessary for [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfixed-size buffers[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Breaking Changes**: The fix only affects the internal string copying logic, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot the external API or protocol dissection behavior[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Reference to Similar Solutions[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe disabled implementation at lines [0m[1;36m3040[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3101[0m[39m demonstrates the correct approach:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m3089[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3091[0m[39m: Length clamping pattern[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Line [0m[1;36m3093[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m3094[0m[39m: Safe copy and null termination[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix adapts that pattern to work with the `out_tvb`-based architecture used by [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe current implementation.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
